T^2 & \vec R_{T^2}\subset R_2 & \text{oriented }R_2\text{-phase}\
T^3 & \vec R_{T^3}=R_3 & \text{complement / half-period}\
T^4 & \vec R_{T^4}\subset R_2 & \text{reverse }R_2\text{-phase}\
